  let x_len = List.length x in
  let y_len = List.length y in
  if x_len <> y_len then false
  else
    let x_iter = List.iter x in
    let y_iter = List.iter y in
    let x_head = List.head x_iter in
    let y_head = List.head y_iter in
    if x_head < y_head then false
    else
      let x_tail = List.tail x_iter in
      let y_tail = List.tail y_iter in
      if x_tail < y_tail then false
      else
        let x_tail_len = List.length x_tail in
        let y_tail_len = List.length y_tail in
        if x_tail_len <> y_tail_len then false
        else
          let x_iter = List.iter x_tail in
          let y_iter = List.iter y_tail in
          let x_head = List.head x_iter in

let f x y =
  let x_len = List.length x in
  let y_len = List.length y in
  if x_len <> y_len then false
  else
    let x_iter = List.iter x in
    let y_iter = List.iter y in
    let x_head = List.head x_iter in
    let y_head = List.head y_iter in
    if x_head < y_head then false
    else
      let x_tail = List.tail x_iter in
      let y_tail = List.tail y_iter in
      if x_tail < y_tail then false
      else
        let x_tail_len = List.length x_tail in
        let y_tail_len = List.length y_tail in
        if x_tail_len <> y_tail_len then false
        else
          let x_iter = List.iter x_tail in
          let y_iter = List.iter y_tail in
          let x_head = List.head x_iter in
          let y_head = List.head y_iter in
          if x_head < y_head then false
          else
            let x_tail = List.tail

 (* Write a function to check if each element of second tuple is smaller than its corresponding element in the first tuple. *)

  let x_len = List.length x in
  let y_len = List.length y in
  if x_len <> y_len then false
  else
